9385|tramp|v. to walk heavily or noisily; n. a person who travels from place to place on foot in search of work or as a vagrant.
9386|only|adj. & adv. and no one or nothing else besides.
9387|teapot|n. a pot with a handle, spout, and lid, in which tea is brewed and from which it is poured.
9388|handicapped|adj. having a condition that markedly restricts their ability to function physically, mentally, or socially.
